  // ── seeded random ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function seededRand(seed) {
    var s = seed;
    return function () {
      s = (s * 1664525 + 1013904223) & 0xffffffff;
      return (s >>> 0) / 0xffffffff;
    };
  }

  function zeroOverride() {
    var o = {};
    state.parties.forEach(function (p) { o[p.key] = 0; });
    return o;
  }

  // ── util ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function clamp(v, lo, hi) { return Math.max(lo, Math.min(hi, v)); }

  // ── color utilities ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function hexToRgb(hex) {
    return [parseInt(hex.slice(1,3),16), parseInt(hex.slice(3,5),16), parseInt(hex.slice(5,7),16)];
  }
  function rgbToHex(r, g, b) {
    return "#" + [r,g,b].map(function(v){ return Math.round(clamp(v,0,255)).toString(16).padStart(2,"0"); }).join("");
  }
  function partyShades(color) {
    var c = hexToRgb(color), r=c[0], g=c[1], b=c[2];
    return [
      rgbToHex(r*0.22+232*0.78, g*0.22+226*0.78, b*0.22+222*0.78),
      rgbToHex(r*0.55+232*0.45, g*0.55+226*0.45, b*0.55+222*0.45),
      color,
      rgbToHex(r*0.58, g*0.58, b*0.58)
    ];
  }
  function escapeHtml(str) {
    return String(str).replace(/&/g,"&amp;").replace(/</g,"&lt;").replace(/>/g,"&gt;").replace(/"/g,"&quot;");
  }

  // ── init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    renderPartyPanel();
    renderScoreGrid();
    renderVoteStrip();
    renderTrendSliders();
    renderBoostButtons();
    bindControls();
    buildMap();
  });

  function bindControls() {
    var ctrls = ["statewideSwing", "turnoutPulse", "metroMomentum", "mountainSwing", "westernSwing", "volatility"];
    ctrls.forEach(function (key) {
      var el = document.getElementById(key);
      var valEl = document.getElementById(key + "-value");
      el.addEventListener("input", function () {
        state.controls[key] = Number(el.value);
        valEl.textContent = Number(el.value).toFixed(1);
        simulateAndRender(false);
      });
    });

    document.getElementById("apply-preset").addEventListener("click", function () {
      var key = document.getElementById("preset-select").value;
      if (key && PRESETS[key]) applyPreset(key);
    });
    document.getElementById("reroll-button").addEventListener("click", function () { simulateAndRender(true); });
    document.getElementById("reset-button").addEventListener("click", resetAll);
    document.getElementById("add-party").addEventListener("click", addParty);
    document.getElementById("reset-parties").addEventListener("click", resetParties);
    document.getElementById("party-list").addEventListener("click", handlePartyListClick);
    document.getElementById("party-list").addEventListener("input", handlePartyListInput);
  }

  function bindTrendSliders() {
    state.parties.forEach(function (p) {
      var key = p.key + "Trend";
      var el = document.getElementById(key);
      var valEl = document.getElementById(key + "-value");
      if (!el) return;
      el.addEventListener("input", function () {
        state.controls[key] = Number(el.value);
        valEl.textContent = Number(el.value).toFixed(1);
        simulateAndRender(false);
      });
    });
  }

  function bindBoostButtons() {
    state.parties.forEach(function (p) {
      var el = document.getElementById("boost-" + p.key);
      if (el) el.addEventListener("click", function () { nudgeSelected(p.key, 5); });
    });
    var resetEl = document.getElementById("reset-region");
    if (resetEl) resetEl.addEventListener("click", clearSelectedOverride);
  }

  // ── party management ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  var PALETTE_OPTIONS = ["#e6194b","#3cb44b","#ffe119","#4363d8","#f58231","#911eb4","#42d4f4","#f032e6","#bfef45","#fabed4"];

  function addParty() {
    var color = PALETTE_OPTIONS[state.nextPartyId % PALETTE_OPTIONS.length];
    var newParty = { key: "party" + state.nextPartyId, label: "P" + state.nextPartyId,
      name: "New Party " + state.nextPartyId, color: color, baseStrength: 10, removable: true };
    state.nextPartyId++;
    state.controls[newParty.key + "Trend"] = 0;
    state.regions.forEach(function (r) {
      r.override[newParty.key] = 0;
      if (r.result) r.result[newParty.key] = 0;
    });
    state.parties.push(newParty);
    onPartiesChanged();
  }

  function resetParties() {
    state.parties = makeDefaultParties();
    state.nextPartyId = 6;
    Object.keys(state.controls).forEach(function (k) { if (k.endsWith("Trend")) delete state.controls[k]; });
    state.controls.ppdTrend = 0; state.controls.pnpTrend = 0;
    state.controls.mvcTrend = 0; state.controls.pipTrend = 0; state.controls.pdTrend = 0;
    state.regions.forEach(function (r) { r.override = zeroOverride(); });
    onPartiesChanged();
  }

  function handlePartyListClick(event) {
    var btn = event.target.closest(".party-remove");
    if (!btn) return;
    var key = btn.getAttribute("data-key");
    if (state.parties.length <= 2) return;
    state.parties = state.parties.filter(function (p) { return p.key !== key; });
    delete state.controls[key + "Trend"];
    state.regions.forEach(function (r) {
      delete r.override[key];
      if (r.result) delete r.result[key];
    });
    onPartiesChanged();
  }

  function handlePartyListInput(event) {
    var el = event.target;
    var key = el.getAttribute("data-key");
    var field = el.getAttribute("data-field");
    if (!key || !field) return;
    var party = state.parties.find(function (p) { return p.key === key; });
    if (!party) return;
    if (field === "baseStrength") {
      party.baseStrength = Number(el.value);
      var valSpan = el.closest(".party-field").querySelector(".party-bs-val");
      if (valSpan) valSpan.textContent = party.baseStrength + "%";
    } else {
      party[field] = el.value;
    }
    renderScoreGrid();
    renderVoteStrip();
    renderTrendSliders();
    renderBoostButtons();
    if (field === "color") renderPartyPanel();
    if (state.regions.length) simulateAndRender(false);
  }

  function onPartiesChanged() {
    renderPartyPanel();
    renderScoreGrid();
    renderVoteStrip();
    renderTrendSliders();
    renderBoostButtons();
    if (state.regions.length) simulateAndRender(false);
  }

  // ── dynamic UI rendering ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderPartyPanel() {
    var container = document.getElementById("party-list");
    container.innerHTML = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      var shades = partyShades(p.color);
      var removeBtn = state.parties.length > 2
        ? '<button class="party-remove" data-key="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" type="button" title="Remove party">\u00d7</button>'
        : "";
      var isCustom = ORIG_KEYS.indexOf(p.key) === -1;
      var strengthField = isCustom
        ? '<label class="party-field"><span class="party-field__row"><span>Base Strength</span><span class="party-bs-val">' + p.baseStrength + '%</span></span>' +
          '<input type="range" data-key="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" data-field="baseStrength" min="1" max="40" step="1" value="' + p.baseStrength + '"></label>'
        : "";
      return [
        '<article class="party-card" data-key="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" style="border-left:4px solid ' + p.color + ';">',
        '<div class="party-card__top">',
        '<div class="party-palette-preview">',
        shades.map(function (s) { return '<span style="background:' + s + ';"></span>'; }).join(""),
        '</div>', removeBtn, '</div>',
        '<div class="party-fields">',
        '<label class="party-field"><span>Label</span><input type="text" data-key="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" data-field="label" value="' + escapeHtml(p.label) + '" maxlength="8"></label>',
        '<label class="party-field"><span>Name</span><input type="text" data-key="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" data-field="name" value="' + escapeHtml(p.name) + '"></label>',
        '<label class="party-field party-field--color"><span>Color</span><input type="color" data-key="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" data-field="color" value="' + p.color + '"></label>',
        strengthField,
        '</div></article>'
      ].join("");
    }).join("");
  }

  function renderScoreGrid() {
    var grid = document.getElementById("score-grid");
    grid.innerHTML = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      var shades = partyShades(p.color);
      return [
        '<div class="score-card" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,' + shades[0] + ',rgba(255,255,255,0.7));border-color:' + shades[1] + ';">',
        '<p class="score-card__label" style="color:' + p.color + ';">' + escapeHtml(p.label) + '</p>',
        '<p class="score-card__value" id="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '-count" style="color:' + p.color + ';">—</p>',
        '<p class="score-card__sub">' + escapeHtml(p.name.split(" ").slice(0,2).join(" ")) + '</p>',
        '</div>'
      ].join("");
    }).join("");
  }

  function renderVoteStrip() {
    var labelsEl = document.getElementById("vote-strip-labels");
    var stripEl  = document.getElementById("vote-strip");
    var w = (100 / state.parties.length).toFixed(1);
    labelsEl.innerHTML = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      return '<span id="' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '-pct-label" style="color:' + p.color + ';font-weight:700;">' + escapeHtml(p.label) + ' 0%</span>';
    }).join("");
    stripEl.innerHTML = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      return '<div class="vote-strip__seg" id="strip-' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" style="background:' + p.color + ';width:' + w + '%;"></div>';
    }).join("");
  }

  function renderTrendSliders() {
    var container = document.getElementById("trend-sliders");
    container.innerHTML = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      var key = p.key + "Trend";
      var val = state.controls[key] !== undefined ? state.controls[key] : 0;
      return [
        '<div class="slider-row">',
        '<div class="slider-row__top">',
        '<span class="slider-row__label" style="color:' + p.color + ';">' + escapeHtml(p.label) + ' Surge</span>',
        '<span class="slider-row__val" id="' + escapeHtml(key) + '-value">' + val.toFixed(1) + '</span>',
        '</div>',
        '<input type="range" id="' + escapeHtml(key) + '" min="-10" max="10" step="0.5" value="' + val + '" style="accent-color:' + p.color + ';">',
        '</div>'
      ].join("");
    }).join("");
    bindTrendSliders();
  }

  function renderBoostButtons() {
    var container = document.getElementById("region-actions");
    container.innerHTML = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      var shades = partyShades(p.color);
      return '<button id="boost-' + escapeHtml(p.key) + '" class="button" style="font-size:0.82rem;background:' + shades[0] + ';border-color:' + shades[1] + ';color:' + p.color + ';">+' + escapeHtml(p.label) + '</button>';
    }).join("") + '<button id="reset-region" class="button button--ghost" style="font-size:0.82rem;">Reset</button>';
    bindBoostButtons();
  }

  function applyPreset(key) {
    var p = PRESETS[key];
    if (!p) return;
    Object.keys(p.controls).forEach(function (k) {
      state.controls[k] = p.controls[k];
      var el = document.getElementById(k); if (el) el.value = p.controls[k];
      var valEl = document.getElementById(k + "-value"); if (valEl) valEl.textContent = Number(p.controls[k]).toFixed(1);
    });
    simulateAndRender(true);
  }

  function resetAll() {
    Object.keys(state.controls).forEach(function (k) {
      var def = (k === "volatility") ? 3 : 0;
      state.controls[k] = def;
      var el = document.getElementById(k); if (el) el.value = def;
      var valEl = document.getElementById(k + "-value"); if (valEl) valEl.textContent = Number(def).toFixed(1);
    });
    state.regions.forEach(function (r) { r.override = zeroOverride(); });
    simulateAndRender(true);
  }

  // ── map build ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function buildMap() {
    var geo = window.PR_GEO;
    if (!geo) { document.getElementById("map-status").textContent = "GeoJSON not loaded."; return; }

    var shell = document.getElementById("map-shell");
    var W = 800, H = 520;
    var projection = d3.geoMercator().fitSize([W, H], geo);
    var pathGen = d3.geoPath().projection(projection);

    var svg = d3.select(shell)
      .append("svg")
      .attr("viewBox", "0 0 " + W + " " + H)
      .attr("aria-label", "Puerto Rico municipality map");

    var muniByName = {};
    MUNIS.forEach(function (m) { muniByName[m.name.toLowerCase()] = m; });

    var defaultMuni = function(name) {
      return { name: name, region: "central", base: { ppd:33, pnp:32, mvc:15, pip:13, pd:7 } };
    };

    var regions = geo.features.map(function (feature) {
      var featureName = (feature.properties.NAME || "").trim();
      var muni = muniByName[featureName.toLowerCase()];
      if (!muni) {
        MUNIS.forEach(function (m) {
          if (!muni && featureName.toLowerCase().indexOf(m.name.toLowerCase().split(" ")[0]) !== -1) muni = m;
        });
      }
      if (!muni) muni = defaultMuni(featureName);
      return { feature: feature, muni: muni, override: zeroOverride(), result: null, path: null };
    });

    state.regions = regions;

    var g = svg.append("g");
    regions.forEach(function (r, i) {
      r.path = g.append("path")
        .datum(r.feature)
        .attr("d", pathGen)
        .attr("data-idx", i)
        .on("mouseenter", function (event) { showTooltip(event, r); })
        .on("mousemove",  function (event) { moveTooltip(event); })
        .on("mouseleave", hideTooltip)
        .on("click",      function () { selectRegion(i); });
    });

    document.getElementById("map-status").textContent = "78 municipalities loaded.";
    simulateAndRender(true);
  }

  // ── simulate ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  // Swing coefficients for original parties (ppd benefits, others lose)
  var SWING_COEFF = { ppd: 1, pnp: -0.6, mvc: -0.2, pip: -0.15, pd: -0.05 };

  function simulateAndRender(reroll) {
    if (reroll) state.seed = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1e9);
    var rand = seededRand(state.seed);
    var c = state.controls;

    state.regions.forEach(function (r) {
      var b = r.muni.base;
      var ov = r.override;

      var sw = c.statewideSwing || 0;
      if (r.muni.region === "metro")    sw += (c.metroMomentum || 0);
      if (r.muni.region === "mountain") sw += (c.mountainSwing || 0);
      if (r.muni.region === "west")     sw += (c.westernSwing  || 0);

      function noise() { return (rand() * 2 - 1) * (c.volatility || 3); }

      var raw = {};
      state.parties.forEach(function (p) {
        var base = (b[p.key] !== undefined) ? b[p.key] : (p.baseStrength || 10);
        var swCoeff = (SWING_COEFF[p.key] !== undefined) ? SWING_COEFF[p.key] : -0.1;
        var trend = c[p.key + "Trend"] || 0;
        raw[p.key] = Math.max(1, base + sw * swCoeff + trend + noise() + (ov[p.key] || 0));
      });

      var total = state.parties.reduce(function (s, p) { return s + raw[p.key]; }, 0);
      var result = {};
      state.parties.forEach(function (p) { result[p.key] = raw[p.key] / total * 100; });
      r.result = result;
    });

    renderMap();
    renderScores();
    renderCloseRaces();
    if (state.selectedId !== null) renderRegionPanel(state.selectedId);
  }

  // ── render map ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function winnerOf(result) {
    var best = null, bestVal = -1;
    Object.keys(result).forEach(function(k){ if (result[k] > bestVal) { bestVal = result[k]; best = k; } });
    return best;
  }

  function partyColor(partyKey, margin) {
    var party = state.parties.find(function (p) { return p.key === partyKey; });
    if (!party) return "#d7cec3";
    var shades = partyShades(party.color);
    if (margin < 3)  return shades[0];
    if (margin < 8)  return shades[1];
    if (margin < 18) return shades[2];
    return shades[3];
  }

  function renderMap() {
    state.regions.forEach(function (r, i) {
      if (!r.result) return;
      var keys = Object.keys(r.result).sort(function(a,b){ return r.result[b]-r.result[a]; });
      var w = keys[0], runnerUp = keys[1];
      var margin = r.result[w] - (r.result[runnerUp] || 0);
      r.path.attr("fill", partyColor(w, margin)).classed("selected", state.selectedId === i);
    });
  }

  // ── vote pie ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function describePieSlice(cx, cy, radius, startAngle, endAngle) {
    var sweep = endAngle - startAngle;
    if (sweep >= Math.PI * 2 - 0.0001) {
      return ["M",cx,cy-radius,"A",radius,radius,0,1,1,cx-0.01,cy-radius,"L",cx,cy,"Z"].join(" ");
    }
    var s = polarToCartesian(cx, cy, radius, startAngle);
    var e = polarToCartesian(cx, cy, radius, endAngle);
    return ["M",cx,cy,"L",s.x.toFixed(2),s.y.toFixed(2),"A",radius,radius,0,sweep>Math.PI?1:0,1,e.x.toFixed(2),e.y.toFixed(2),"Z"].join(" ");
  }
  function polarToCartesian(cx, cy, radius, angle) {
    return { x: cx + Math.cos(angle) * radius, y: cy + Math.sin(angle) * radius };
  }

  function renderVotePie(partyShares) {
    var size = 208, cx = 104, cy = 104, r = 82;
    var angle = -Math.PI / 2;
    var winner = partyShares[0];
    var defName   = winner ? winner.party.label : "—";
    var defShare  = winner ? winner.pct.toFixed(1) + "%" : "—";
    var defDetail = winner ? winner.party.name.split(" ").slice(0, 3).join(" ") : "Hover a slice";

    var slices = partyShares.map(function(e) {
      var sweep = (e.pct / 100) * Math.PI * 2;
      var end = angle + sweep;
      var d = describePieSlice(cx, cy, r, angle, end);
      angle = end;
      var lbl = e.party.label + ": " + e.pct.toFixed(1) + "%";
      return '<path class="vote-pie__slice" d="' + d + '" fill="' + e.party.color + '"' +
        ' data-pie-name="' + escapeHtml(e.party.label) + '"' +
        ' data-pie-share="' + e.pct.toFixed(1) + '%"' +
        ' data-pie-detail="' + escapeHtml(e.party.name) + '"' +
        ' aria-label="' + escapeHtml(lbl) + '" tabindex="0"><title>' + escapeHtml(lbl) + '</title></path>';
    }).join("");

    return '<div class="vote-pie-wrap">' +
      '<div class="vote-pie" id="vote-pie"' +
      ' data-default-name="' + escapeHtml(defName) + '"' +
      ' data-default-share="' + escapeHtml(defShare) + '"' +
      ' data-default-detail="' + escapeHtml(defDetail) + '">' +
      '<svg class="vote-pie__svg" viewBox="0 0 ' + size + ' ' + size + '" aria-label="Vote share pie chart">' +
      slices + '</svg></div>' +
      '<div class="vote-pie__readout">' +
      '<span class="vote-pie__eyebrow" id="pie-eyebrow">' + escapeHtml(defDetail) + '</span>' +
      '<strong class="vote-pie__label" id="pie-label">' + escapeHtml(defName) + '</strong>' +
      '<span class="vote-pie__share" id="pie-share">' + escapeHtml(defShare) + '</span>' +
      '</div></div>';
  }

  function updatePie(partyShares) {
    var container = document.getElementById("pie-container");
    container.innerHTML = renderVotePie(partyShares);
    var pie = container.querySelector(".vote-pie");
    if (!pie) return;
    pie.addEventListener("mouseover", function(ev) {
      var slice = ev.target.closest("[data-pie-name]");
      if (!slice) return;
      document.getElementById("pie-eyebrow").textContent = slice.getAttribute("data-pie-detail") || "";
      document.getElementById("pie-label").textContent   = slice.getAttribute("data-pie-name")   || "";
      document.getElementById("pie-share").textContent   = slice.getAttribute("data-pie-share")  || "";
    });
    pie.addEventListener("mouseleave", function() {
      document.getElementById("pie-eyebrow").textContent = pie.getAttribute("data-default-detail") || "";
      document.getElementById("pie-label").textContent   = pie.getAttribute("data-default-name")   || "";
      document.getElementById("pie-share").textContent   = pie.getAttribute("data-default-share")  || "";
    });
  }

  // ── render scores ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderScores() {
    var wins = {}, votes = {};
    state.parties.forEach(function (p) { wins[p.key] = 0; votes[p.key] = 0; });

    state.regions.forEach(function (r) {
      if (!r.result) return;
      var w = winnerOf(r.result);
      if (w !== null && wins[w] !== undefined) wins[w]++;
      state.parties.forEach(function (p) { votes[p.key] += (r.result[p.key] || 0); });
    });

    var totalVotes = state.parties.reduce(function (s, p) { return s + votes[p.key]; }, 0);

    var partyShares = state.parties.map(function (p) {
      return { party: p, pct: totalVotes ? votes[p.key] / totalVotes * 100 : 0 };
    }).sort(function (a, b) { return b.pct - a.pct; });
    updatePie(partyShares);

    state.parties.forEach(function (p) {
      var el = document.getElementById(p.key + "-count");
      if (el) el.textContent = wins[p.key];
      var pct = totalVotes ? votes[p.key] / totalVotes * 100 : 0;
      var stripEl = document.getElementById("strip-" + p.key);
      if (stripEl) stripEl.style.width = pct.toFixed(1) + "%";
      var lblEl = document.getElementById(p.key + "-pct-label");
      if (lblEl) lblEl.textContent = p.label + " " + pct.toFixed(1) + "%";
    });

    var banner = document.getElementById("winner-banner");
    var topKey = Object.keys(wins).sort(function (a, b) { return wins[b] - wins[a]; })[0];
    var topWins = wins[topKey];
    var tied = Object.keys(wins).filter(function (k) { return wins[k] === topWins; });
    if (tied.length > 1) {
      banner.textContent = "Tight race \u2014 no clear leader";
      banner.style.background = "rgba(200,139,45,0.15)";
      banner.style.color = "#5a3c10";
      banner.style.border = "1px solid rgba(200,139,45,0.3)";
      banner.className = "winner-banner";
    } else {
      var p = state.parties.find(function (pp) { return pp.key === topKey; });
      if (p) {
        var rgb = hexToRgb(p.color);
        banner.textContent = p.label + " leads with " + topWins + " municipalities";
        banner.style.background = "rgba(" + rgb[0] + "," + rgb[1] + "," + rgb[2] + ",0.12)";
        banner.style.color = rgbToHex(rgb[0]*0.45, rgb[1]*0.45, rgb[2]*0.45);
        banner.style.border = "1px solid rgba(" + rgb[0] + "," + rgb[1] + "," + rgb[2] + ",0.25)";
        banner.className = "winner-banner";
      }
    }
  }

  // ── close races ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderCloseRaces() {
    var sorted = state.regions.filter(function (r) { return r.result; }).map(function (r) {
      var keys = Object.keys(r.result).sort(function(a,b){ return r.result[b]-r.result[a]; });
      return { name: r.muni.name, winner: keys[0], margin: r.result[keys[0]] - (r.result[keys[1]] || 0) };
    }).sort(function(a,b){ return a.margin - b.margin; }).slice(0,8);

    var container = document.getElementById("close-races");
    container.innerHTML = "";
    sorted.forEach(function (c) {
      var p = state.parties.find(function(p){ return p.key === c.winner; });
      if (!p) return;
      var div = document.createElement("div");
      div.className = "race-item";
      div.innerHTML =
        '<span class="race-item__swatch" style="background:' + p.color + '"></span>' +
        '<span class="race-item__name">' + c.name + '</span>' +
        '<span class="race-item__margin">' + p.label + ' +' + c.margin.toFixed(1) + '%</span>';
      container.appendChild(div);
    });
  }

  // ── region panel ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function selectRegion(i) {
    state.selectedId = (state.selectedId === i) ? null : i;
    renderMap();
    if (state.selectedId !== null) {
      renderRegionPanel(state.selectedId);
      document.getElementById("region-panel").classList.remove("is-hidden");
    } else {
      document.getElementById("region-panel").classList.add("is-hidden");
    }
  }

  function renderRegionPanel(i) {
    var r = state.regions[i];
    document.getElementById("region-title").textContent = r.muni.name;
    var keys = Object.keys(r.result).sort(function(a,b){ return r.result[b]-r.result[a]; });
    var winner = keys[0], margin = r.result[keys[0]] - (r.result[keys[1]] || 0);
    var p = state.parties.find(function(p){ return p.key === winner; });
    var hasOverride = Object.values(r.override).some(function(v){ return v !== 0; });
    document.getElementById("region-summary").textContent =
      (p ? p.label : winner) + " leads +" + margin.toFixed(1) + "% \u2022 " + r.muni.region +
      (hasOverride ? " \u2022 local override active" : "");
  }

  function nudgeSelected(partyKey, pts) {
    if (state.selectedId === null) return;
    var ov = state.regions[state.selectedId].override;
    ov[partyKey] = clamp((ov[partyKey] || 0) + pts, -25, 25);
    var others = state.parties.map(function(p){ return p.key; }).filter(function(k){ return k !== partyKey; });
    others.forEach(function(k){ ov[k] = clamp((ov[k] || 0) - pts / others.length, -25, 25); });
    simulateAndRender(false);
  }

  function clearSelectedOverride() {
    if (state.selectedId === null) return;
    state.regions[state.selectedId].override = zeroOverride();
    simulateAndRender(false);
  }

  // ── tooltip ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  var tooltipEl = document.getElementById("map-tooltip");
  var ttTitle   = document.getElementById("tt-title");
  var ttMeta    = document.getElementById("tt-meta");
  var ttCands   = document.getElementById("tt-candidates");

  function showTooltip(event, r) {
    ttTitle.textContent = r.muni.name;
    ttMeta.textContent  = "Region: " + r.muni.region;
    var res = r.result || r.muni.base;
    var sorted = state.parties.slice().sort(function(a,b){ return (res[b.key]||0)-(res[a.key]||0); });
    ttCands.innerHTML = sorted.map(function(p){
      return candidateLine(p.label, res[p.key] || 0, p.color);
    }).join("");
    tooltipEl.removeAttribute("hidden");
    moveTooltip(event);
  }

  function candidateLine(name, pct, color) {
    return '<div class="candidate-line">' +
      '<span class="candidate-line__swatch" style="background:' + color + '"></span>' +
      '<span>' + name + '</span>' +
      '<span class="candidate-line__pct">' + pct.toFixed(1) + '%</span>' +
      '</div>';
  }

  function moveTooltip(event) {
    var stage = document.querySelector(".map-stage");
    var rect  = stage.getBoundingClientRect();
    var x = event.clientX - rect.left + 12;
    var y = event.clientY - rect.top  + 12;
    if (x + 280 > rect.width)  x = event.clientX - rect.left - 280;
    if (y + 120 > rect.height) y = event.clientY - rect.top  - 120;
    tooltipEl.style.left = x + "px";
    tooltipEl.style.top  = y + "px";
  }

  function hideTooltip() {
    tooltipEl.setAttribute("hidden", "");
  }

}());
</script>


</body></html>
